In [25]: def th2th_N_plan(N,step,offset):
    ...:     """
    ...:     N = section number
    ...:     start(N=0) = 1
    ...:     overlap=1.5
    ...:     range size = 2.25 = (55-1)/12
    ...:     """
    ...:     start=(N-1)*2.25+1
    ...:     stop=N*2.25+1+1.5
    ...:     npts=int((stop-start)/step+1)
    ...:     yield from bp.scan([scaler,D4calc],kth_motor,start+offset,stop+offset,tth_motor,start*2,stop*2,npts)
    ...:
